                "ccpa-opt-out-lspa": "true",
            }
        };
        const BANNER_SDK = {
            url: "https://cdn.cookielaw.org/scripttemplates/202404.1.0/otBannerSdk.js",
            options: {},
        }

        const countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {"countries":["ES","MX","PH","TH","TR"]};

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">Mera Mera no Mi</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Flame-Flame Fruit (<a href="/wiki/VIZ_Media" title="VIZ Media">VIZ</a>, <a href="/wiki/Funimation" title="Funimation">Funimation</a>);<br>Flare-Flare Fruit (<a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a>, Funimation subs)</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Sound of fire burning</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a></div>
</div>

</section>
</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible" style="color: #FDA81B;">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: #DE362C">Devil Fruit</th></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">Mera Mera no Mi</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Flame-Flame Fruit (<a href="/wiki/VIZ_Media" title="VIZ Media">VIZ</a>, <a href="/wiki/Funimation" title="Funimation">Funimation</a>);<br>Flare-Flare Fruit (<a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a>, Funimation subs)</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Sound of fire burning</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>"Ace" redirects here. For Roger's sword which went by the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Ace_(Sword)" title="Ace (Sword)">Ace (Sword)</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Portgas D. Ace</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> born as <b>Gol D. Ace</b><sup id="cite_ref-Rouge_Names_Ace_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rouge_Names_Ace-6">[6]</a></sup> and nicknamed <b>"Fire Fist" Ace</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-Hiken_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hiken-5">[5]</a></sup> was the biological son of the late Pirate King, <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Rouge" title="Portgas D. Rouge">Portgas D. Rouge</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-parentage_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-parentage-12">[12]</a></sup> as well as the <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki_(Ceremony)#Brothers'_Sake_Cups" title="Sakazuki (Ceremony)">sworn</a> older brother of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a><sup id="cite_ref-BrotherhoodAge_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BrotherhoodAge-7">[7]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> Ace was first adopted by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a>, as had been requested by Roger before his execution.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> Ace was <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Spade_Pirates" title="Spade Pirates">Spade Pirates</a><sup id="cite_ref-Spade_Pirates_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spade_Pirates-3">[3]</a></sup> before being recruited into the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and becoming its 2nd division <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates#Division_Commanders" title="Whitebeard Pirates">commander</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-recognition_by_Smoker_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-recognition_by_Smoker-2">[2]</a></sup> He ate the <a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">Mera Mera no Mi</a>, giving him the power to transform into and manipulate flames.
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, a member of his division, committed the unforgivable crime of murdering a <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">crewmate</a> and fleeing, Ace went on a quest to hunt him down. When Ace finally found Blackbeard, though, a <a href="/wiki/Duel_on_Banaro_Island" title="Duel on Banaro Island">heated duel</a> resulted in Ace's defeat, allowing Blackbeard to turn him in to the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. Worried about his lineage and wanting to make an example, the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> sentenced Ace to death, which resulted in the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, an all-out clash of powers between <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>'s forces and the combined might of the Marines and the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords</a>. Ace was freed,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> but before he could escape <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>, he sacrificed his life to protect Luffy from <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a>, thanking Luffy and his friends for loving him before dying peacefully in his brother's arms."<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>Ace's death ultimately proved to be the catalyst leading to Luffy training for two years to become strong enough to protect his <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">friends</a>, paving the way for the <a href="/wiki/The_Final_Sea:_The_New_World_Saga" title="The Final Sea: The New World Saga">second half of the series</a>. His reincarnated Devil Fruit would eventually be consumed by his sworn brother, Sabo, ensuring that his <a href="/wiki/Inherited_Will" title="Inherited Will">will would live on</a>.
</p><p>Ace was first shown during the <a href="/wiki/Drum_Island_Arc" title="Drum Island Arc">Drum Island Arc</a>, but only got formally introduced in the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a>, where he acts as a brief ally of the Straw Hat Pirates. He is a central figure during the whole <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_Saga" title="Summit War Saga">Summit War Saga</a>. He is also the protagonist of <a href="/wiki/Ace%27s_Great_Blackbeard_Search" title="Ace's Great Blackbeard Search">Ace's Great Blackbeard Search</a> Cover Page Serial.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">
	</div>
	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8252" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">Who are the biological parents of Portgas D. Ace?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						The biological parents of Portgas D. Ace are Gol D. Roger, the Pirate King, and Portgas D. Rouge. Rouge, who resided in South Blue, carried Ace in her womb for an extraordinary 20 months and sadly passed away after giving birth. Despite Ace initially claiming Whitebeard as his father, his true lineage was revealed by the World Government.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8253" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of Ace's tattoo in One Piece?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Ace's tattoo in One Piece holds significant meaning. The tattoo on his back is a symbol of his pride and joy, representing his allegiance to Whitebeard, whom he viewed as a father figure. Additionally, Ace has another tattoo on his upper left bicep that spells 'ASCE' vertically. The 'S' crossed out is a tribute to Sabo, indicating his jolly roger. This tattoo is a symbol of the bond between Ace, Luffy, and Sabo.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8254" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">Who adopted Portgas D. Ace and why?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Portgas D. Ace was adopted by Monkey D. Garp, who is also the grandfather of Monkey D. Luffy. Garp decided to adopt Ace because of his unique lineage. Ace is the son of Gol D. Roger, the King of the Pirates. To protect Ace from the government and those who would harm him due to his father's reputation, Garp took him in and raised him as his own.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8255" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What was Ace's role in the Whitebeard Pirates?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Portgas D. Ace played a significant role in the Whitebeard Pirates. Initially, he was the captain of the Spade Pirates and was even offered a position as a Shichibukai, which he turned down. After a failed attempt to kill Whitebeard, he was offered a place in the Whitebeard Pirates and became a division commander. Ace was highly regarded and had authority over lower-ranking subordinates. He was one of the strongest pirates on board, under Whitebeard himself. However, when Blackbeard betrayed the crew, Ace left on a mission to capture him, showcasing his loyalty and dedication to the crew.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8256" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How does Portgas D. Ace meet his end in the series?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In the thrilling world of One Piece, Portgas D. Ace meets his end in a heroic and heartbreaking way. He was captured and set to be executed at Marineford, which sparked a massive battle as his allies, including the Whitebeard Pirates, fought to save him. Despite their efforts, Ace was tragically killed, marking a significant and emotional point in the series. His death is covered in detail in Chapter 574 and Episode 483 of the anime, and his memory continues to impact the characters and storyline.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
	</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Ace was a tall muscular young man with jaw-length curly black hair. Although they were not blood related, Ace looked remarkably like his foster brother, Luffy. However, Ace was more serious looking than Luffy's lighthearted design, and was also taller and more muscular. He also sported rather childish freckles (inherited from his mother) and tended to make a skeptical facial expression by raising his left eyebrow. Interestingly, his facial features were almost akin to his biological father Gol D. Roger in his youth without his mustache.
</p><p>Ace's tattoos were among his most remarkable, trademark features. He had a tattoo on his back of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates#Jolly_Roger" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard symbol</a>—purple bones formed in a cross behind a purple skull with a white mustache—that he described as his pride and joy.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> Ace had another tattoo on his upper left bicep that spells "A<del>S</del>CE" vertically. The "S" crossed out is a tribute to <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> as that's his jolly roger.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> On the cover of <a href="/wiki/Chapter_596" title="Chapter 596">Chapter 596</a> indeed, Ace's tattoo is written as "ACE" instead of the original "A<del>S</del>CE" as the cover is a "what if" image of Ace, Luffy, and Sabo together as adults with the former being known to be alive.
</p><p>Ace wore an open-front shirt until he received Whitebeard's tattoo - afterwards, he stopped wearing anything over his upper body except when on winter or desert islands due to the weather requirements. He wore black boots, black knee-length shorts with an eyelet-studded orange belt, and a blue pouch belted around his left leg. He also wore a short second belt with a large red "A" on the silver buckle over his right hip, but left it unfastened and threaded the free end along the back of his shorts. A dagger in a green sheath hung at his left hip. On Ace's left arm, he wore a <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Pose</a> and a red and white striped bracelet around his wrist, an orange elbow guard, and his "ASCE" tattoo. He wore a red beaded necklace and an orange hat with two blue <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger#Smileys" title="Jolly Roger">smileys</a>, one frowning and one smiling, and a string of red beads sitting above the rim. Two long orange side straps hung down sides of his hat and met at a large medallion of a bull's skull with orange tassels.
</p><p>Unfortunately, Ace lost his trademark hat, which he already had when he began his journey as a pirate, on <a href="/wiki/Banaro_Island" title="Banaro Island">Banaro Island</a> as a result of his duel with Blackbeard. His knife and log pose was also apparently confiscated, as he no longer had it in his next appearance as a prisoner at <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>. The tattoo upon his back that he took so much pride in was later destroyed by the same blow that eventually led to his death. However, at his grave, Ace's hat and knife were placed at his tombstone—either they were retrieved, or they were duplicates in Ace's possession.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p><p>During the ending credits in the second movie, <i><a href="/wiki/Clockwork_Island_Adventure" title="Clockwork Island Adventure">Clockwork Island Adventure</a></i>, previews of upcoming characters from the Baroque Works Saga were featured. Ace was also included amongst the many characters, but while his clothes were almost identical, he boasted a very different color scheme to the one he was given in his official appearance in the anime.
</p><p>As a child, Ace is shown to have often worn t-shirts with two-kanji phrases on the front (such as "innocence" and "violence"). On some occasions they are linked to the scene in which they were worn, like "independence" when the three brothers built their own tree house to live in. He often wore knee-length shorts and a black elbow guard on his left arm. Ace was always seen wearing dark brown, flat, slipper-like shoes, and in the winter, he wore a green cardigan over his normal clothes.
</p><p>Upon leaving <a href="/wiki/Dawn_Island" title="Dawn Island">Dawn Island</a> at the age of 17, he wore an outfit identical to the one he wore when he first met Whitebeard; however, he was less muscular than he eventually grew to be and had rounder, more childlike facial features.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Series">Main Series</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 130px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 130px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4f/Save_My_Heart.png/revision/latest?cb=20171009155710" class="image"><img alt="Save My Heart" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="108" height="108" data-image-name="Save My Heart.png" data-image-key="Save_My_Heart.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4f/Save_My_Heart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/108?cb=20171009155710" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace on the cover of the disc <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Island_Song_Collection" title="One Piece Island Song Collection">One Piece Island Song Collection</a></i>.

</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Ace was much more intelligent, polite, and generally, more bearable than <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>, which prompted the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> to question whether he was truly related to their captain. While several people who knew <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> noted Luffy is quite similar to the late <a href="/wiki/Pirate#Pirate_King" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a>, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> himself claimed that Ace's personality was not at all like his father's. It seems that among the very few things the brothers shared was their recklessness as pirates (and their near-bottomless stomachs). In addition, Ace liked to party as much as his brother does. When he boarded <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a>'s ship, he was drawn by the smell of food and decided to enjoy himself while he was there. Ace could be a bit inappropriate though as he once used a woman's skirt to wipe his face while he was dining at Spice Bean in Arabasta.
</p><p>There were two running gags about Ace. The first was his rather extreme narcolepsy. He tended to randomly fall asleep while eating and conversing, leaving strangers around him wondering if he had died. This was first seen in <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta</a> when they thought he died in the middle of eating. The second was that he did a "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/dine_and_dash" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:dine and dash">dine and dash</a>" routine wherever he went. This went back to his younger days with <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> and Luffy, when they would often dine and dash in the city of <a href="/wiki/Goa_Kingdom" title="Goa Kingdom">Goa</a>, and carried over to adulthood, as shown on three occasions when he was on <a href="/wiki/Drum_Island" title="Drum Island">Drum Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lulusia_Kingdom" title="Lulusia Kingdom">Lulusia Kingdom</a>.
</p><p>Ace was also shown to be quite impulsive, much like his younger brother, as he too would make hasty decisions and, in some cases, neglect listening to reason. This was shown that shortly prior to setting out to hunt Blackbeard for killing Thatch. Whitebeard insisted that Ace should not go after him, yet Ace, despite his immense loyalty and respect for his captain, ignored his warnings and went off to find his former subordinate. Another, albeit more humorous example, was in his mini-story, where during his hunt for Blackbeard, he mistook a man named Dr. Blackbeard for his target, due to coincidentally having a similar name and appearance to Teach. Rather than check to see if he found the man he was looking for, Ace jumped to conclusions too soon and attacked the doctor on sight. It was by then Ace realized too late that he had the wrong man, which got him into a lot of trouble with the villagers.
</p><p>His "politeness" is due to <a href="/wiki/Makino" title="Makino">Makino</a>'s teaching after Ace asked her how to introduce himself to <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> (being his <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">brother</a>'s savior).<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> Before that, Ace was rather cold and rude to anyone he was not familiar with.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p><p>As the son of Roger, he lived in his shadow and is to date the first <a href="/wiki/Will_of_D." title="Will of D.">D.</a> depicted to truly question his own right to exist, while displaying the fewest commonly seen D. related traits. Ace seemed to have lifelong problems dealing with his parentage, even after denouncing Gol D. Roger and accepting Whitebeard as his only father. This was in direct contrast to Luffy, who accepted his father's identity immediately upon learning it and did not seem to care when he was told how dangerous of a man he was. However, Luffy did not grow up with knowledge of the identity (or even the existence) of his father. Ace believed that it was natural if he were to really die as nobody in the world wanted the son of the devil (Roger) to live. This caused him to be surprised and shocked that Whitebeard would easily accept him in his crew despite him being the son of Whitebeard's rival and that the entire Whitebeard Pirates' crew and allies and Luffy would risk their lives in order to save him. Ace commented upon his own death that he had never sought fame or fortune - all he had wanted was the answer to his lifelong question of whether or not he should have been born, as this was the only thing preventing him from dying with no regrets as he and Luffy had vowed to do so and the fact he had a younger brother to look out for. Ace's only regret was that he would not live to see Luffy achieve his dream, which he believed Luffy undoubtedly would accomplish as he was his little brother.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Benn_Beckman" title="Benn Beckman">Benn Beckman</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> described Ace's personality to be naiver than his appearance would suggest. He compared Ace's characteristics to be more aligned with the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>'s, considering his personal vendetta against the world denying his existence. Ace is described to be more of a fighter than a Pirate, making Beckman think Ace is unfit to be captain of a fleet.<sup id="cite_ref-nA2_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nA2-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>Ace had a tendency to never back down from a fight, saying that he would never run once facing an enemy. Also like his father and brother, Ace was confident and fearless when confronting his opponents even when they were extremely powerful people such as Whitebeard or admirals like Aokiji or Akainu, though like Luffy, he could also underestimate his opponents. When Blackbeard demonstrated the power of the <a href="/wiki/Yami_Yami_no_Mi" title="Yami Yami no Mi">Yami Yami no Mi</a>, Ace was unfazed, not viewing it as a threat to himself and only showed shock and fear when Teach used his power to grab him and cancel his Devil Fruit powers. He also tried to kill Whitebeard at least a hundred times despite the massive difference in strength between them and each of his attempts failing miserably. Because of this, some people believed that Ace had a death wish, but in truth, he wanted to prevent the people he cared for from getting hurt. <a href="/wiki/Curly_Dadan" title="Curly Dadan">Dadan</a> stated that he inherited this tendency from his father despite loathing him. While Ace emerged victorious over enemies he refused to run from, such as <a href="/wiki/Porchemy" title="Porchemy">Porchemy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bluejam" title="Bluejam">Bluejam</a>, his stubbornness hurt him on a number of occasions, particularly when he refused to back down against <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> or <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a>.
</p><p>Ace was also easily provoked by and became violent towards anyone who insulted or harmed people close to him. In one of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a>'s conversations with Curly Dadan, this was revealed to be a trait of Roger as well. During his childhood, Ace had a tendency to severely injure anyone who insulted Roger, though he himself disliked his biological father. After hearing about Sabo's presumed death at the hands of a World Noble, Ace quickly became bent on killing the Noble and Dadan had to pin Ace down and tie him to a tree to stop him.
</p><p>Ace's temper got the better of him, especially in cases when Whitebeard, proclaimed by Ace to be his only father, was insulted. Believing that this was the case when <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> broke the iron rule of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and fled after murdering a <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">crewmate</a>, Ace pursued his traitorous subordinate despite his crewmates' efforts and even Whitebeard's orders to stop him. Ace later came to see that his stubbornness had gotten him into the ordeal of being scheduled for execution. Even though he managed to escape death on the scaffold thanks to the pirates' and Luffy's efforts at <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> and was well on his way to freedom, Admiral Akainu got to him by insulting Whitebeard. Ace quickly turned back to face him, ignoring his crewmates' warnings to not become angered over Akainu's provocations. Unwilling to let him get away of speaking ill of Whitebeard, Ace attacked him out of fury only to have his arm burned by Akainu's Devil Fruit powers. Akainu then took the opportunity to attack Luffy on the sideline, leading Ace to jump in, sacrificing his life to shield Luffy from the attack. While saying his last words, Ace sadly admitted to Luffy that he (Ace) wasted away all of his efforts to rescue him.
</p><p>Although Ace follows the creed of loyalty towards those close to him, such as taking the excessive effort to rescue Luffy from Bluejam or hunting down Teach to avenge Thatch, he was not above using underhanded methods to win a fight at times. Noted examples included trying to stab Whitebeard in his sleep or chopping him down with an axe from behind.
</p><p>Alongside his loyalty is Ace does not judge people by their appearance and <a href="/wiki/Race" title="Race">race</a>, but by their character, as he took in both <a href="/wiki/Ganryu" title="Ganryu">Ganryu</a> (a <a href="/wiki/Longarm_Tribe" title="Longarm Tribe">Longarm</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Wallace" title="Wallace">Wallace</a> (a <a href="/wiki/Fish-Men" title="Fish-Men">Fish-Man</a>) into his crew while society had shunned both of them.
</p><p>Ace was very generous toward those that had very little to eat and willing to share his own food with them. On Sixis, he kindly offered the first <a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">fruit</a> he found to a starving Masked Deuce, despite being hungry himself, an act that made Masked Deuce feel ashamed since he was planning on killing Ace for the food. When the Spade Pirates arrived in Wano Country and the starving locals tied them up and took their food, Ace kindly asked them if they wanted dessert, When he learned the terrible living conditions were caused by Kaidou, Ace wanted to kill the Emperor so the people wouldn't go hungry again.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crews">Crews</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whitebeard_Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">I will make Whitebeard...the King.</td>

<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20230917230828" class="image"><img alt="Ace Bows to Whitebeard" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace Bows to Whitebeard.png" data-image-key="Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230917230828"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20230917230828" class="image"><img alt="Ace Bows to Whitebeard" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230917230828" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace Bows to Whitebeard.png" data-image-key="Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230917230828"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_Bows_to_Whitebeard.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace bows to Whitebeard in their final moments together.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace initially intended to take <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>'s head but was defeated. Whitebeard invited him to be <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">one of his sons</a>, which Ace vehemently refused; despite this, Whitebeard abducted the entire <a href="/wiki/Spade_Pirates" title="Spade Pirates">Spade Pirates</a> onto his crew.
</p><p>After trying to assassinate Whitebeard many times, Ace was eventually drawn in by <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a>'s description of the love the Whitebeard Pirates bore for their father. He decided to give up on his struggles and take up Whitebeard's symbol on his back; this tattoo became his greatest pride and joy.<sup id="cite_ref-Ace_the_pirate_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ace_the_pirate-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>Ace held great respect for his captain. As far as Ace was concerned, Whitebeard was the greatest pirate alive, and even went so far as to describe Whitebeard as a type of father figure.
</p><p>Ace was a loyal crewman and commanded the 2nd division of the Whitebeard Pirates. It is revealed that <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">Thatch</a> was one of the first of Whitebeard's crew to interact with him and they appear to have been good friends. Ace and Marco also seemed to have a close friendship due to Marco explaining the bond between Whitebeard and his crew. <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>, who later became Blackbeard, once served as a member of the 2nd division under Ace and they are shown eating together in flashback with Blackbeard encouraging Ace to become 2nd commander. The Whitebeard Pirates were revealed to be very fond of Ace and unhesitatingly vowed to rescue him from his execution, as seen when they shouted out that they would not forgive anyone who hurt him.
</p><p>Whitebeard seemed unconcerned about Ace's hunt for Blackbeard and remained grounded that it was Ace's duty to execute the traitor, regardless of the heavy warnings he received from <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>. It was revealed however that Whitebeard himself was troubled about Ace hunting Blackbeard and gave him no such orders, but Ace stubbornly set out anyways to hunt down his traitorous former subordinate. Even so, Whitebeard took responsibility for Ace's decision and claimed that it was under his orders that Ace went after Blackbeard.
</p><p>Whitebeard immediately mobilized his crew and his subordinate crews after hearing about Ace's imminent execution. The Whitebeard Pirates reached <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>, along with many allied powerful pirate crews, and were at war with the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> and <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Spade_Pirates">Spade Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ace was extremely loyal to the <a href="/wiki/Spade_Pirates" title="Spade Pirates">Spade Pirates</a>, the crew that he formed himself. When he knew that they stood no chance against <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, he formed a firewall to allow them to escape, leaving himself behind to hold Whitebeard back alone. The Spade Pirates also share this loyalty and looked up to their captain fondly as Ace gave each of them a place on his ship regardless of their races or appearances. When Ace was fighting <a href="/wiki/Isuka" title="Isuka">Isuka</a>, his crew members rushed in to help, even though they were unable to hit her.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup> Despite their earlier thrashing at the hands of Whitebeard, they challenged the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> in the hopes of retrieving their captain but were soundly beaten and abducted along with him.<sup id="cite_ref-Ace_the_pirate_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ace_the_pirate-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_novel_A" title="One Piece novel A">novel</a> about Ace, Ace seemed to share a particular bond with <a href="/wiki/Masked_Deuce" title="Masked Deuce">Masked Deuce</a>, who he met while stranded on an island with no apparent means of escape. The two initially started on cold terms when Deuce continued to turn down Ace's approaches to be friends, which was further strained when he learned that Ace was the son of the Pirate King. However, he later came to accept Ace and helped form the Spade Pirates together with him, and remarked that he, like the other crew members, viewed Ace like the sun.<sup id="cite_ref-nA2_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nA2-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Ace was recruiting his crew members, he recognized <a href="/wiki/Skull" title="Skull">Skull</a>'s experience and knowledge of pirates, finding value in his subordinate's pirate fascination. Ace also supported <a href="/wiki/Mihar" title="Mihar">Mihar</a>'s passion for helping children. When Ace found <a href="/wiki/Kotatsu" title="Kotatsu">Kotatsu</a> injured from a poacher's trap, he saved the lynx. Because of this, Kotatsu's cowardly personality became courageous. He also loved to sit next to Ace, as his captain's Devil Fruit abilities kept him warm.<sup id="cite_ref-nA1_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nA1-27">[27]</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Spade_Pirates" title="Spade Pirates">Spade Pirates</a>, who are now a part of Whitebeard's crew, mourned his death.
</p>
