<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png/revision/latest?cb=20160707164354" class="image"><img alt="Ace and Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="229" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace and Luffy Fighting Against Marine Officers.png" data-image-key="Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160707164354"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png/revision/latest?cb=20160707164354" class="image"><img alt="Ace and Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160707164354" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="229" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace and Luffy Fighting Against Marine Officers.png" data-image-key="Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160707164354"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_and_Luffy_Fighting_Against_Marine_Officers.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace and Luffy's last battle together.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace and his brother, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>, were very close as children and remained so as pirates, even after more than three years of separation. Though they were not related by blood, they were still bound by a brotherly bond. Luffy was also aware that Ace was <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s son. As a child, Ace was initially aloof and hostile towards Luffy. Such an example was when Luffy innocently followed Ace onto an old rope bridge and Ace (being greatly annoyed by his presence) knocked Luffy off the bridge and into the ravine. After learning how lonely Luffy was, Ace warmed up to him, but got annoyed whenever Luffy cried. Ace later grew very protective of him, particularly from <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a>, even insulting their grandfather in an attempt to stop his abusive behavior towards Luffy. This protective streak continued into the current storyline. Ace first intervened to protect Luffy from <a href="/wiki/Smoker" title="Smoker">Smoker</a> in <a href="/wiki/Nanohana" title="Nanohana">Nanohana</a>. Later, when he discovered that <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> meant to kill Luffy and hand him over to the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, Ace immediately warned him that he would not let him lay a finger on his little brother. Despite their closeness, Luffy often made Ace angry and frequently worried him by doing reckless things.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup> It was because of this that Ace did not doubt <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a> when she informed him that Luffy had infiltrated <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> to rescue him. Another instance would be when Ace was being transported to <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>. He was however, constantly worrying about Luffy's welfare, repeatedly saying his name and thinking about him.
</p><p>Though frequently worried by Luffy's extravagant recklessness, inwardly Ace seemed quite proud of his brother's past exploits; in the anime, he was shown grinning slightly as he listened to Garp, visiting him in prison, discussing Luffy's ruckus-raising on <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup> Apparently, Ace had been known to frequently share stories about Luffy with the other ranks of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>. He was quite overjoyed when he learned that Luffy had gained his first bounty and wasted no time showing the wanted poster to <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> himself. After Luffy's unceremonious entrance into the fray at <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> had no trouble identifying him as the brother Ace was always talking about, even prior to Luffy loudly declaring it for all to hear.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup> Even when he made a new friend in <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>, he apparently frequently boasted to him about Luffy, to the point where they got tired of it.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p><p>Ace tended to portray a typical good-big-brother behavior, such as asking the Straw Hat crew to keep an eye on his little brother. He also ensured Luffy had a way of meeting up with him by giving him a <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Card</a>. They respected each other's choices despite their differences and understood that the other was strong enough to look after himself. Luffy believed that if he grew worried about Ace and rushed to his aid, Ace's ego would not allow it, so he initially left him alone even after discovering that Ace was hurt via the Vivre Card. However, when he learned that Ace had been captured and was due for execution and saw that Ace's Vivre Card had burnt down to a tenth of its original size, Luffy decided take a side trip and save Ace instead of sailing directly from <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a> to reunite with his crew.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913094501" class="image"><img alt="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="207" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper.png" data-image-key="Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220913094501"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913094501" class="image"><img alt="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220913094501" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="207" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper.png" data-image-key="Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220913094501"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace,_Dragon,_Garp,_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace appears on the news about Luffy's return.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace's protectiveness of his brother was seen again when both the Whitebeard Pirates and Luffy had invaded <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> in order to save him and he told Luffy to turn back. Luffy refused and pressed on while proclaiming he would save him. Ace was later surprised at Luffy's ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Hakii</a> and realized his brother had a potential that he was not aware of. After Luffy freed him, the two fought by each other's side and Ace did not even hesitate to throw his life away to save Luffy as he leaped in the way to shield his brother from Akainu as the admiral struck. Ace's only regret was that he would not live to see Luffy achieve his dream, which he believed Luffy undoubtedly would. Ace passed on smiling, while Luffy collapsed into mindless grief over his beloved brother's death. In fact, one of the reasons why the Whitebeard Pirates would defend Luffy is because he is Ace's beloved brother.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sabo">Sabo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> was Ace's good friend and brother from ten years ago. They had planned to become pirates by saving money to buy a pirate ship, a joint attempt that began five years before Luffy followed Ace to the Gray Terminal and to Sabo. Sabo was one of the two people Ace considered a brother along with Luffy. They performed an informal <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki_(Ceremony)#Brothers'_Sake_Cups" title="Sakazuki (Ceremony)">sakazuki ceremony</a> together to seal their bond as brothers. When Sabo sacrificed his happiness to save Ace's and Luffy's lives from his <a href="/wiki/Outlook_III" title="Outlook III">father</a>'s wrath, Ace decided to forget Sabo for the moment, thinking that if Sabo were happy, then he and Luffy should be proud. However, after Sabo was presumably killed at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Jalmack" title="Jalmack">Saint Jalmack</a>, Ace regretted his previous decision, flew into a rage, and attempted to kill the noble in revenge, but was stopped by Dadan, and later wept at the apparent loss of his brother, despite earlier claiming to Luffy that men should not cry. Before dying, Ace mentioned Sabo as one of the reasons that ever made him want to live in the first place.
</p><p>Ace had a tattoo on his upper left bicep that spells "A<del>S</del>CE" vertically. The "S" crossed out is a tribute to Sabo as that was his jolly roger.
</p><p>Tragically enough, Sabo survived this event but because he had amnesia, he could not reveal himself to Ace or Luffy. Ace died without ever knowing that Sabo was alive the entire time.
</p><p>Shortly after Ace's death, Sabo regained his memories and later visited his grave before he went on to inherit his brother's <a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">power</a> to carry on his memory.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Portgas_D._Rouge">Portgas D. Rouge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Rouge" title="Portgas D. Rouge">Rouge</a> was Ace's mother, who carried him in her womb for 20 months in order to protect the innocent child from the clutches of the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-parentage_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-parentage-12">[12]</a></sup> Ace was born one year and three months after Roger's death, therefore Rouge was five months pregnant when she resorted to some unknown method (assumed by <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> to be sheer willpower) to postpone birth. Just before passing away, Rouge gave him the name Gol D. Ace.<sup id="cite_ref-Rouge_Names_Ace_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rouge_Names_Ace-6">[6]</a></sup> However, Ace, grateful to his mother for her sacrifice, chose to take her name instead.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gol_D._Roger">Gol D. Roger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>It has been revealed that Ace's father was the Pirate King, <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, contrary to the previous belief that his father was <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-parentage_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-parentage-12">[12]</a></sup>
</p><p>Before Ace was born, Roger requested Garp to watch over him on his behalf. However, Ace felt that he did not owe him anything, which is why he preferred the name of his mother, who died protecting him. The reason for this was because Roger had a reputation as a "devil" among the general population, which led them to hate, despise and curse the possibility of the existence of a son of Roger, causing Ace to hate his father for bringing him into a world that wanted him dead for the simple fact of existing. Although Ace resented his father, he brutally beat up anyone who spoke ill of him.
</p><p>To this date, Ace was the one of the few pirates shown to speak ill of Gol D. Roger, along with <a href="/wiki/Squard" title="Squard">Squard</a>, though many unnamed pirates on Level 6 of <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> were known to have grudges against the late Pirate King.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Prior to <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> making it public to the world, Ace knew that Dragon is Luffy's father. Other than that, it is unknown what Ace thought about him and vice-versa. During a talk with Garp, Ace brought up the fact that both he and Luffy share the blood of infamous criminals.
</p><p>It is also unknown if Dragon knew that Ace was the son of Roger (before this fact was made known to the world by Sengoku) or if he was aware of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">his father</a> adopting Ace, though Dragon's closer subordinate <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> did at least know that Ace was Luffy's older brother by adoption.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Garp">Monkey D. Garp</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest?cb=20230601052749" class="image"><img alt="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition.png" data-image-key="Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230601052749"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest?cb=20230601052749" class="image"><img alt="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230601052749" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition.png" data-image-key="Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230601052749"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace and Garp at Marineford.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> adopted Ace as a favor to Roger to give Ace a life free of the prejudice of being born from a family of pirates.
</p><p>Though he did come to see Garp as family, he did not approve of his violent behavior towards Luffy. At one point he warned him to stop abusing Luffy going as so far to call him an "old piece of crap". Garp, who had promised to make fine Marines out of the two brothers,<sup id="cite_ref-c556_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c556-36">[36]</a></sup> was furious when he discovered that Ace had gone ahead to become a pirate instead.<sup id="cite_ref-Ace_the_pirate_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ace_the_pirate-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>Though respectful of his "grandfather", Ace announced that he and Luffy would never have become <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> even if they wanted to. He disagreed with Garp and remains grounded on the idea that becoming Marines would not have been possible since both of their fathers were world class criminals. Garp, in return, showed extreme sadness about Ace's execution, and cried about Ace's choice in a life of piracy and declared Ace as family. Garp was also willing to kill <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a> for killing Ace. When Ace was dying, he thanked Garp for loving him and the latter broke down when his grandson finally died.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Curly_Dadan">Curly Dadan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Curly_Dadan" title="Curly Dadan">Curly Dadan</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Bandits#Mountain_Bandits" title="Bandits">mountain bandit</a> who was blackmailed by Garp, became the foster mother for Ace and Luffy. Whenever Ace would nearly kill villagers for insulting his heritage, Dadan would get angry at the boy for his actions, to which Ace would snidely remark that he regrets that his victims did not die. Dadan also shows weariness at dealing with Ace, and gives the impression that she would refuse if not for Garp holding her gang's crimes over her head. However, when the Nobles of Goa burned the Grey Terminal, Dadan led her bandits into the inferno to find Ace, Luffy and Sabo and when Ace refused to back down from confronting Bluejam, Dadan had the bandits take Luffy to safety while she stayed behind to stand beside Ace. The two really care for each other as Dadan saved Ace from being burned and Ace was willing to steal medicine from town in order to treat Dadan's wounds. When Ace set out to become a pirate, she was sulking when she heard Ace's message that he was grateful to her. Ace seemed to like Dadan, and prior to his death, asked Luffy to tell her goodbye on his behalf and that he misses her. Although Dadan outwardly viewed and treated Ace as a nuisance that she wanted gone, she actually loved and cared about him a lot. When she discovered Ace's death, she buried her sorrows in drinks and furiously attacked Garp when he returned for not doing anything to save Ace, accusing him of having chosen work above family.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends">Friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shanks">Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Ace_Meets_Shanks.png/revision/latest?cb=20230520060822" class="image"><img alt="Ace Meets Shanks" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace Meets Shanks.png" data-image-key="Ace_Meets_Shanks.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Ace_Meets_Shanks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230520060822"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Ace_Meets_Shanks.png/revision/latest?cb=20230520060822" class="image"><img alt="Ace Meets Shanks" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Ace_Meets_Shanks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230520060822" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace Meets Shanks.png" data-image-key="Ace_Meets_Shanks.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Ace_Meets_Shanks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230520060822"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_Meets_Shanks.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace meets Shanks.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>, was on relatively good terms with Ace, who seemed to greatly respect him primarily for his role in saving his adoptive younger brother, Luffy, from the <a href="/wiki/Lord_of_the_Coast" title="Lord of the Coast">Lord of the Coast</a> during the incident with <a href="/wiki/Higuma" title="Higuma">Higuma</a>. After setting out to begin his life of piracy, Ace immediately sought out Shanks to meet the man in person and thank him on Luffy's behalf. Shanks was initially hostile until he learned Ace's reasons, and the two even celebrated their meeting. Shanks showed some concern for Ace upon learning that he was in pursuit of <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>. He personally sought out <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> to vocally disapprove and attempted to persuade Whitebeard to recall Ace. After the announcement of Ace's execution, it was revealed that Shanks personally intercepted <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, another of the Four Emperors, as the latter attempted to take advantage of the crisis and attack Whitebeard. It is unknown if Shanks ever discovered that Ace was the son of his late captain Gol D. Roger (before this fact was made public by Sengoku).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Buggy_and_Alvida_Alliance">Buggy and Alvida Alliance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/26/Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png/revision/latest?cb=20230806175845" class="image"><img alt="Ace at Buggy Pirates party" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace at Buggy Pirates party.png" data-image-key="Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/26/Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230806175845"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/26/Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png/revision/latest?cb=20230806175845" class="image"><img alt="Ace at Buggy Pirates party" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/26/Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230806175845" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace at Buggy Pirates party.png" data-image-key="Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/26/Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230806175845"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_at_Buggy_Pirates_party.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace convinces <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> to join his <a href="/wiki/Buggy_Pirates" title="Buggy Pirates">crew</a>'s party.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During his pursuit of <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, Ace happened across the <a href="/wiki/Big_Top" title="Big Top">Big Top</a> while <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> and his crew were partying. Attracted by the "very strong and sweet scent" of food, Ace boarded the ship unnoticed and proceeded to help himself - Buggy did not notice his presence until, upon hearing Buggy and Alvida say that they were in pursuit of Luffy but had no clue where he was, Ace offered to give them some helpful information. Ace, being Ace, fell asleep moments later. Though Buggy's crew wanted to capture him, Buggy forbade it, knowing that Whitebeard would not hesitate to take revenge. After Ace woke up, the entire crew apparently enjoyed the rest of his momentary stay.
</p><p>Buggy himself seems to like Ace as after meeting Luffy on Level One, he mentions that Ace, unlike Luffy, happened to be a very swell guy and they were apparently drinking buddies for a while. Buggy also told Luffy that he was very upset when he heard the news of Ace's scheduled execution. Like so many at the time, Buggy was shocked to see Ace fall to Admiral Akainu.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ace and <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> were once enemies, as Ace wanted to kill Whitebeard, whom Jinbe regarded as a hero for protecting Fish-Man Island. The two dueled for five days until they both collapsed from exhaustion. Despite this scuffle, the two eventually became friends who deeply respected each other. During their time in Impel Down, they were cellmates and Ace asked Jinbe to take care of Luffy after he died, a wish that Jinbe at first refused despite their friendship as Jinbe did not feel like protecting anyone whom he considered to be a stranger. This changed when he developed respect for Luffy and when Ace truly did die.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> Jinbe was more than willing to forfeit his status as <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a> to battle for Ace's freedom and shed tears for Ace's demise.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ace was on good terms with Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">crew</a> after they met in <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta</a>. The crew took a liking to Ace and questioned if he and Luffy were related given the former's politeness. Before parting ways, Ace entrusted them to look after Luffy.
</p><p>At <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> was excited to see Ace himself. When Ace's <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Card</a> in Luffy's possession began to burn, <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> was concerned about Ace's well-being.
</p><p>After the battle at <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> during the Straw Hats' separation, they were gravely alarmed upon learning of his death. This led to them being deeply concerned about Luffy's well-being given how close they were, and he died in front of him before he suffered a mental breakdown.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tama">Tama</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Roughly a year during his pirating journey, Ace arrived to the <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> region in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, where he encountered a young girl named <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Tama</a>. They shared a strong bond that inspired Tama to become a Kunoichi. After Ace promised to return to visit her, Tama waited for him despite the terrible living conditions caused by the Beasts Pirates. When Luffy informed her of Ace's death, Tama was deeply upset and refused to believe him.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> She was later surprised to learn that Luffy was his younger brother.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Yamato">Yamato</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629132940" class="image"><img alt="Yamato Drinks WIth Ace" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Yamato Drinks WIth Ace.png" data-image-key="Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629132940"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629132940" class="image"><img alt="Yamato Drinks WIth Ace" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629132940" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Yamato Drinks WIth Ace.png" data-image-key="Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629132940"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Yamato_Drinks_WIth_Ace.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Yamato sharing drinks with Ace.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace had met <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a> roughly four years before the current storyline. While the two initially clashed, they quickly got along and drank together.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> During this time Ace told Yamato about his younger brother Luffy and before they parted ways gifted him a Vivre card.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> Yamato greatly respects Ace, as he fondly stated that Luffy reminds him of the former and that while he could not leave Onigashima with Ace, he would set sail on Luffy's ship due to them being brothers. Yamato revealed to Luffy he had originally wanted to sail out of Wano with Ace, but his father's handcuffs kept him prisoner on Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Isuka">Isuka</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_novel_A" title="One Piece novel A">novel</a>, Ace and <a href="/wiki/Isuka" title="Isuka">Isuka</a>'s relationship was similar to Luffy and Smoker's relationship, except on more amicable terms. She attacked Ace and his crew, viewing it as her duty to enforce justice. When she almost drowned, Ace threw her a life preserver, causing her to change her view about him. She attacked his crew several times since then, but Ace easily dealt with her with no grudges. Isuka then decided to try to get Ace to give up piracy, seeing him as a good person. After Ace stopped Draw's assault, Ace offered her a spot in his crew but she declined and parted ways with him on good terms.<sup id="cite_ref-nA1_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nA1-27">[27]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marshall_D._Teach">Marshall D. Teach</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ace's main enemy was <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>, also known as "Blackbeard". Prior to his betrayal, Ace and Teach were on good terms, with the latter encouraging him to be commander after he declines the position.
</p><p>Once Teach betrayed Whitebeard, Ace personally chose to hunt down for killing <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">Thatch</a>. However, as <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> stated, Ace was strong and young, but the fact that he was appointed as Whitebeard's Second Division commander worried Shanks due to "that trust and reputation" getting in the way. Shanks concluded that Ace was not ready to face Blackbeard, which was confirmed later when Ace confronted him and his crew. At first, Blackbeard wanted him to join and hunt down Luffy, but Ace declined his offer and the two fought against each other. In the end, Ace was defeated and turned in to the Marines, thus granting Blackbeard the status of <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Smoker">Smoker</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316022040" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Meets Portgas D" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker Meets Portgas D. Ace.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230316022040"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316022040" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Meets Portgas D" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230316022040" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker Meets Portgas D. Ace.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230316022040"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_Meets_Portgas_D._Ace.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace meets Smoker in the <a href="/wiki/Spice_Bean" title="Spice Bean">Spice Bean</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>They met in Arabasta when <a href="/wiki/Smoker" title="Smoker">Smoker</a> was hunting for Luffy but found Ace instead. He tried to arrest the Whitebeard Commander though both were conveniently sent flying by Luffy. Smoker soon ignored Ace and went after Luffy, something that caused Ace to intervene on his brother's behalf.
</p><p>Smoker questioned Ace's reason before he was informed, they were brothers. Ace also fought evenly with Smoker for a few moments, who even Luffy has yet to beat. The elements of their <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a> <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a> canceled each other out, and neither of them were able to gain the upper hand even though Ace was just trying to gain some time for the Straw Hats to get away.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, after discovering that Ace was the son of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, desired to execute him but was unable to touch him due to Ace joining Whitebeard's crew. When Blackbeard defeated and turned him in, they seized the chance and made Ace's execution their highest priority. It appeared that Ace shared a similar fate with <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> and Luffy - his sole existence was a sin to the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, being the child of the "world's greatest evil".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Akainu">Akainu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a> earned Ace's scorn for badmouthing Whitebeard as Ace and Luffy were making their retreat, provoking Ace to turn back and let his chance to escape <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> slip away. He attacked Akainu in fury over the insult but discovered that his fire was inferior to that of Akainu's magma. Akainu was able to burn Ace and eventually kill him.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">But you had to be stopped. In time your abilities would eventually allow you to lead a new generation of pirates on a reign of terror! For this reason, your execution today is necessary! Even if it means all-out war with Whitebeard!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Sengoku on Ace's potential and why his execution had to carry out.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>As commander of the 2nd division of the Whitebeard Pirates, Ace had authority over the lower-ranking subordinates. In addition, as one of the top commanders of the Whitebeard Pirates, he was one of the strongest and most highly regarded pirates on board under <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> himself. 
</p><p>At one point, while being captain of the Spade Pirates, he was even asked to join the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> but refused.<sup id="cite_ref-c552p6_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c552p6-43">[43]</a></sup> Even as a rookie, Ace was powerful enough to defeat <a href="/wiki/Hanafuda" title="Hanafuda">Hanafuda</a>, a Warlord, resulting in him losing his position and likely contributing to Ace's prior invitation.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> Ace was strong enough to be acknowledged by the Emperors Shanks and Blackbeard, with the former saying he had earned his spot as Whitebeard's 2nd division commander and the latter wishing Ace had joined his crew and emphasizing how his own formidable crew was nowhere near strong enough to combat Ace at the time, speaking volumes about Ace's strength.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup> In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_episode_A" title="One Piece episode A">One Piece episode A</a></i>, during the 100th duel between Ace and Whitebeard, <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> remarked on how much stronger Ace had become since their own duel.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy commented on how he never defeated Ace in a single fight, despite Luffy already having the power of the <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">Gomu Gomu no Mi</a> (Ace did not consume the <a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">Mera Mera no Mi</a> until after he left: Luffy was surprised by Ace's new power when Ace stopped Smoker from capturing him in <a href="/wiki/Nanohana" title="Nanohana">Nanohana</a>). Ace was trained by Garp, who had hoped to turn him into a fine Marine, and possibly Dadan, the two of whom were responsible for training Luffy to the level of power he held before becoming a pirate.
</p><p>Ace also held a fearsome reputation. When he was 10 years old, Ace had already made a name for himself in <a href="/wiki/Gray_Terminal" title="Gray Terminal">Gray Terminal</a>, being known by the <a href="/wiki/Bluejam_Pirates" title="Bluejam Pirates">Bluejam Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup> It was revealed that Ace received an invitation to join the Seven Warlords of the Sea while he was still captain of the Spade Pirates, though he refused the offer, which had subsequently raised his bounty over <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>100,000,000 and attracted even more attention to him across the New World.<sup id="cite_ref-c552p6_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c552p6-43">[43]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-nA2_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nA2-23">[23]</a></sup> He had defeated <a href="/wiki/Doma" title="Doma">Doma</a>, a notorious New World pirate, and his pirate crew all on his own, which is what got him recommended for his current post as the Whitebeard Pirates' 2nd division commander.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup> Due to Ace's prestige and heritage, the World Government not only granted Blackbeard the position of Warlord for successfully defeating and capturing Ace<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> but also imprisoned Ace in Level 6 of <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>, a secret level reserved for the world's most dangerous and brutal criminals.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> His overall reputation and abilities had earned him a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>550,000,000 prior to his capture and death.
</p><p>According to Sengoku, Ace had especially immense potential, described that it was Ace's rapid rise in power and fame that made the World Government realize he was son of the late Pirate King, Gol D. Roger. He went on to say that in time, Ace could potentially become the next Pirate King if he continued on, which was the most important reason why the World Government was willing to start a war with Whitebeard.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> Chinjao himself said that Ace showed the most potential among the new generation pirates, and that his death was a good thing for the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> Before his death, Yamato believed Ace was the one Oden foretold would defeat <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> someday.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p><p>He was also a capable navigator, as he was seen wearing a <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Pose</a> on his left wrist, while traveling from island to island in search of Luffy and Blackbeard on a <a href="/wiki/Striker" title="Striker">simple raft</a>. This also shows he was a skilled tracker.
</p><p>Ace's willpower was strong enough to withstand Shanks' outburst of Supreme King Haki.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133002" class="image"><img alt="Ace Carries Curly Dadan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="286" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace Carries Curly Dadan.png" data-image-key="Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629133002"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133002" class="image"><img alt="Ace Carries Curly Dadan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629133002" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="286" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace Carries Curly Dadan.png" data-image-key="Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629133002"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_Carries_Curly_Dadan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace's immense strength as a child.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Aside from the powers granted by the Devil Fruit he consumed, Ace possessed immense physical strength and endurance which he attained from the extremely rigorous training in the harsh environment of <a href="/wiki/Mt._Colubo" title="Mt. Colubo">Mt. Colubo</a> that consisted of him hunting and fighting wild beasts since childhood and traveling in precarious trap-filled locations. His incredible physical prowess was supplemented by his extraordinary fighting skills. Even in his early childhood, he was able to beat some local thugs who spoke ill of his father "half to death" and during his first meeting with Luffy, he was also shown sitting on top of a huge bull he killed with his staff. As a child, he could also easily break a giant tree with a single kick. In his childhood, before he acquired the Mera Mera no Mi, Ace was able to beat Luffy in every single sparring match, despite Luffy's untrained Gomu Gomu no Mi abilities.
</p><p>Ace demonstrated his strength during his battle with Blackbeard: he was able to take Blackbeard's punches, which were so powerful that the first made Ace cough up blood and the second nearly broke his neck and retaliate quickly afterwards. <a href="/wiki/Van_Augur" title="Van Augur">Van Augur</a> noted that, as expected of the Whitebeard Pirates' 2nd division commander, Ace's basic combat skills were quite formidable even without his Devil Fruit powers.
</p><p>He had shown to fight equally with both <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a> and Jinbe in the past, both being situations where his adversaries used Haki (and in addition in Jinbe's case, Fish-Man Karate) to nullify Ace's Logia powers. Ace and Jinbe in particular had nearly killed each other in a fight that lasted for five days straight. Ace then survived a battle with Whitebeard that took place immediately after, showing immense stamina and durability. As a testament to his stamina and endurance, he was one of the <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">few</a> <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">people</a> to be able to take a "baptizing" in boiling water in <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> without flinching, which is considered an impressive feat.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Mera_Mera_no_Mi" title="Mera Mera no Mi">Mera Mera no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png/revision/latest?cb=20231118091907" class="image"><img alt="Mera Mera no Mi in Use" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mera Mera no Mi in Use.png" data-image-key="Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231118091907"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png/revision/latest?cb=20231118091907" class="image"><img alt="Mera Mera no Mi in Use" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231118091907" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mera Mera no Mi in Use.png" data-image-key="Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231118091907"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mera_Mera_no_Mi_in_Use.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace utilizing the power of the Mera Mera no Mi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace ate the Mera Mera no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allowed him to create, control, and transform his body into fire. He could create and unleash massive amounts of fire for large-scale damage, as well as utilize small precision attacks. Later, after his death, it was revealed that Ace's burning fists also had the power to annihilate entire cities.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup>
</p><p>Ace primarily used his flames for a wide variety of offenses. He could shoot fire bullets and spears, release powerful fire cannons, unleash massive waves of fire, and create fire balls, both a single large one for large-scale destruction and multiple small ones that could explode. His signature attack was transforming his fist into fire and sending it forward as it greatly increased in size, earning him the name "Fire Fist Ace".<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup>
</p><p>His flames could also be used defensively, he could create a massive wall of flames to block his opponents, and the heat of his flames could deter his opponents from attacking him for fear of getting burned. He was also able to stop <a href="/wiki/Hie_Hie_no_Mi" title="Hie Hie no Mi">powerful ice attacks</a> from <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marine</a> <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a>.
</p><p>Ace also had practical uses for his Devil Fruit powers; he would heat up any fish he would find in the seas for his crew when they had no food to eat and he was able to traverse the seas in a <a href="/wiki/Striker" title="Striker">one-man boat</a> that was specifically designed for him and propelled with flames from his feet.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Ace was one of the very few people in the world who could use all three types of Haki. Despite this, he rarely used them in combat, being more reliant on his Devil Fruit abilities. While Ace has never shown usage of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> or <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a> within the manga, the novels have stated that Ace's Haki had been described by <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Benn_Beckman" title="Benn Beckman">Benn Beckman</a> to be fiery in nature, to the point that Ace’s very presence was able to stop blizzards on an island for as long as he was there.<sup id="cite_ref-nA2_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nA2-23">[23]</a></sup> As such, when he turned up on Drum Island, no snow fell at all on the island for an entire day.<sup id="cite_ref-Drum_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Drum-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Supreme_King_Haki">Supreme King Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20220711184301" class="image"><img alt="Ace Uses Supreme King Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="152" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace Uses Supreme King Haki.png" data-image-key="Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220711184301"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20220711184301" class="image"><img alt="Ace Uses Supreme King Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220711184301" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="152" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace Uses Supreme King Haki.png" data-image-key="Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220711184301"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_Uses_Supreme_King_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace unleashes Supreme King Haki for the first time.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace possessed <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, which he initially had no conscious control over. He first demonstrated the ability at 10 years of age when he rendered the <a href="/wiki/Bluejam_Pirates" title="Bluejam Pirates">Bluejam Pirates</a> except for Bluejam unconscious after an outburst of rage.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> He later gained knowledge of the power, as he recognized it when Luffy used it at the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>.
</p><p>He was never seen using this Haki apart from in his childhood, save for in video games (such as during the activation of his Kizuna Rush in <i><a href="/wiki/Pirate_Warriors_3" class="mw-redirect" title="Pirate Warriors 3">Pirate Warriors 3</a></i>) and <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_episode_A" title="One Piece episode A">One Piece episode A</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>It was stated in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_novel_A" title="One Piece novel A">One Piece novel A</a></i> that Ace could use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, though this was not seen within the manga. Upon awakening it, he was capable of fighting on equal grounds with Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Draw" title="Draw">Draw</a> with Armament Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup> However, it is not known how proficient he was in using it since then, though the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_episode_A" title="One Piece episode A">manga adaptation of the novel</a> suggests he was skilled at it, to the point he leaned on it too much and was negligent in training the other forms of his Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-ea3_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ea3-61">[61]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ace has never demonstrated <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a> in the manga or the novel, nor has he been confirmed to have it in the databooks. However, in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_episode_A" title="One Piece episode A">One Piece episode A</a></i>, Ace was trained by <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">Thatch</a> in its usage and used it in his duels against Whitebeard.<sup id="cite_ref-ea3_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ea3-61">[61]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Ace carries around a knife but is never seen using it. However, in flashbacks of attempts to assassinate Whitebeard, Ace was shown using various weapons, including an axe and a knife. As a child, he used a long bo staff made from pipe as a weapon.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Burning_Blood" title="One Piece: Burning Blood">One Piece: Burning Blood</a>, Ace wields two twin double-barreled firearms (which resemble a cross between a pistol and a sawed-off shotgun) while wearing his Strong World costume which he uses as part of his <i>Twin Guns &amp; Cross Fire</i> special attack.
</p>
