<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arabasta_Arc">Arabasta Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When Ace first meets Luffy's crew, he tosses them a <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">piece of paper</a> and leaves. However, in the anime, his time with the Straw Hats was extended and he journeys with them for a while. During the journey though, Ace's bead necklace kept appearing and disappearing in-between scene changes, most likely due to mistakes from the animators.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mera_Mera_no_Mi">Mera Mera no Mi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the manga, it is unknown if Ace can light things on fire from a distance without spouting flames that make direct contact. However, in the anime, he is shown lighting a cigarette for Sanji simply by pointing his finger.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ambition">Ambition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During his meeting with Shanks in the anime, Ace stated that he would become the Pirate King. At no point in the manga did Ace show this ambition, and later he would aim to make <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> the Pirate King. Also in the anime, Ace stated that he wanted to show the world his power by taking Whitebeard's head. Ace's reason for going after Whitebeard's head was never explained in the manga.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Impel_Down_Arc">Impel Down Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133012" class="image"><img alt="Ace and Luffy Non-Canon Appearance" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace and Luffy Non-Canon Appearance.png" data-image-key="Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629133012"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133012" class="image"><img alt="Ace and Luffy Non-Canon Appearance" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629133012" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace and Luffy Non-Canon Appearance.png" data-image-key="Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240629133012"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_and_Luffy_Non-Canon_Appearance.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ace - as depicted in <a href="/wiki/Episode_439" title="Episode 439">Episode 439</a> as a ten-year-old child. (Note the resemblance to his appearance as an adult)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In Episode 439, Ace is depicted as a child similarly to how he appeared as an adult. While in the manga, Ace is almost always wearing a tank top during his childhood, in this episode he is depicted without a shirt, and is seen wearing a red beaded necklace identical to what he wore as an adult. This can be considered a contradiction to the manga, as Ace didn't start wearing his necklace until he was a teenager, and only stopped wearing shirts when he joined the Whitebeard Pirates in order to showcase his "pride and joy" - Whitebeard's Jolly Roger. It can be presumed that Toei Animation did this because Ace's actual childhood appearance hadn't been revealed yet in the manga.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the anime, Ace and Luffy's fight against the Marines (after Luffy unlocked Ace's handcuffs) was expanded and Ace showed more of his attacks.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Death">Death</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Throughout the manga, the anime adaptation, and the specials <a href="/wiki/3D2Y" title="3D2Y"><del>3D</del>2Y</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_of_Sabo" title="Episode of Sabo">Episode of Sabo</a>, Ace's death has been somewhat censored and slightly changed.
</p><p>In the anime, when Ace was struck through by Akainu, his beaded necklace broke apart and fell all over the ground, and one bead ended up rolling to Whitebeard's foot, who picked it up tearfully. In the manga, as well as the specials, the necklace remained intact.
</p><p>In the anime, Ace also was covered in less blood than in the manga and the specials. The anime and 3D2Y also omitted the smoke coming from his wound. In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Romance_Dawn:_The_Dawn_of_the_Adventure" title="One Piece Romance Dawn: The Dawn of the Adventure">Romance Dawn PSP game</a> and its cutscene, Ace only had smoke coming from his wound and the blood was absent.
</p><p>Other oddities include most of the artwork being largely uninspired by the manga.
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Ace%27s_Bloody_Chin_in_the_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20220716171721" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Bloody Chin in the Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="116" data-image-name="Ace's Bloody Chin in the Manga.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Bloody_Chin_in_the_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Ace%27s_Bloody_Chin_in_the_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20220716171721" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's chin covered blood in the manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Ace%27s_Bloody_Chin_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133048" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Bloody Chin in the Anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="68" data-image-name="Ace's Bloody Chin in the Anime.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Bloody_Chin_in_the_Anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Ace%27s_Bloody_Chin_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20240629133048" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's chin showing only thin streaks of blood in the anime version.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Ace%27s_Bloody_Death_in_the_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133040" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Bloody Death in the Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="81" height="120" data-image-name="Ace's Bloody Death in the Manga.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Bloody_Death_in_the_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Ace%27s_Bloody_Death_in_the_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/81?cb=20240629133040" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's death in the manga, which shows more blood and his wound still smoldering.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Ace%27s_Unbloody_Death_in_Episode_483.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133054" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Unbloody Death in Episode 483" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="68" data-image-name="Ace's Unbloody Death in Episode 483.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Unbloody_Death_in_Episode_483.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Ace%27s_Unbloody_Death_in_Episode_483.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20240629133054" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's death in the anime that hardly shows any blood at all.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Ace%27s_Bloody_Death_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20230403230115" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Bloody Death in the Anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="71" data-image-name="Ace's Bloody Death in the Anime.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Bloody_Death_in_the_Anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Ace%27s_Bloody_Death_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20230403230115" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">The following episode, however, increases the amount of blood.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Ace_Dies_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133100" class="image"><img alt="Ace Dies in the Anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="68" data-image-name="Ace Dies in the Anime.png" data-image-key="Ace_Dies_in_the_Anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Ace_Dies_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20240629133100" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">In the anime, Ace's beaded necklace was destroyed moments before his death.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Ace_Dies.png/revision/latest?cb=20230829015022" class="image"><img alt="Ace Dies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="68" data-image-name="Ace Dies.png" data-image-key="Ace_Dies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Ace_Dies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20230829015022" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">In the manga and the specials, his necklace is still intact.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110324094826" class="image"><img alt="POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif" data-image-key="POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20110324094826"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110324094826" class="image"><img alt="POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20110324094826" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif" data-image-key="POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20110324094826"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POPNeoDX-Ace-DomeTourLimited.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Portraits of Pirates Limited Portgas D. Ace.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ace has been a choice character in many forms of merchandise. He has been featured in the <a href="/wiki/Portrait_of_Pirates" title="Portrait of Pirates">Portrait of Pirates</a> <a href="/wiki/Figuarts_ZERO_One_Piece" title="Figuarts ZERO One Piece">Figuarts Zero</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_DX_Figure" title="One Piece DX Figure">One Piece DX Figure</a>, <a href="/wiki/S.H._Figuarts_One_Piece" title="S.H. Figuarts One Piece">S.H. Figuarts One Piece</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_High_Spec_Coloring_Figure" title="One Piece High Spec Coloring Figure">One Piece High Spec Coloring Figure</a>, <a href="/wiki/Master_Stars_Piece" title="Master Stars Piece">Master Stars Piece</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Styling_Figures" title="One Piece Styling Figures">One Piece Styling Figures</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Digital_Grade" title="One Piece Digital Grade">One Piece Digital Grade</a> and <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Super_Effect" title="One Piece Super Effect">One Piece Super Effect</a> Lines.
</p><p>He is also in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Full_Color_R_Gashapon" title="One Piece Full Color R Gashapon">One Piece Full Color R Gashapon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Heroes:_One_Piece" title="Heroes: One Piece">Anichara Heroes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ichiban_Kuji_One_Piece" title="Ichiban Kuji One Piece">Ichiban Kuji</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Logbox" title="One Piece Logbox">One Piece Logbox</a> <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_World_Collectable_Figure" title="One Piece World Collectable Figure">World Collectable</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Attack_Motions" title="One Piece Attack Motions">One Piece Attack Motions</a>, <a href="/wiki/Super_Modeling_Soul_One_Piece" title="Super Modeling Soul One Piece">Super Modeling Soul One Piece</a>, <a href="/wiki/Half_Age_Characters_One_Piece" class="mw-redirect" title="Half Age Characters One Piece">Half Age Characters One Piece</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chibi-Arts_One_Piece" class="mw-redirect" title="Chibi-Arts One Piece">Chibi-Arts One Piece</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Super_Deformed_Figures" title="One Piece Super Deformed Figures">One Piece Super Deformed Figures</a>, <a href="/wiki/Deformeister_Petit_One_Piece" title="Deformeister Petit One Piece">Deformeister Petit One Piece</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Gashapon_Grand_Battle" title="One Piece Gashapon Grand Battle">One Piece Gashapon Grand Battle</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Super_Effect" title="One Piece Super Effect">One Piece Super Effect</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Full_Color_R_Gashapon" title="One Piece Full Color R Gashapon">One Piece Full Color R Gashapon</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Amazing_Log_Collection" title="One Piece Amazing Log Collection">One Piece Amazing Log Collection</a>, <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Full_Face_Jr." title="One Piece Full Face Jr.">One Piece Full Face Jr.</a> and <a href="/wiki/CharaColleCan" title="CharaColleCan">CharaColleCan</a> series.
</p><p>Ace has also featured on several keychains/cellphone straps sets, including the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Desert_Kingdom_Mascot_Keychain/Cellphone_Strap" title="One Piece Desert Kingdom Mascot Keychain/Cellphone Strap">One Piece Desert Kingdom Mascot Keychain/Cellphone Strap</a> collection, alongside his brother Luffy. He even appeared in crossover Merchandise like <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Capsule_Neo_-_Weekly_Shounen_Jump_40_Years_Limited_Edition_with_One_Piece" class="mw-redirect" title="Dragon Ball Capsule Neo - Weekly Shounen Jump 40 Years Limited Edition with One Piece">Dragon Ball Capsule Neo - Weekly Shounen Jump 40 Years Limited Edition with One Piece</a> and <a href="/wiki/Co-Starring_of_Dream!!_Dragon_Ball_Z_x_One_Piece" title="Co-Starring of Dream!! Dragon Ball Z x One Piece">Co-Starring of Dream!! Dragon Ball Z x One Piece</a>.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-Playable_Appearances">Non-Playable Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Treasure_Wars" title="One Piece: Treasure Wars">One Piece: Treasure Wars</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D57&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a></i>, it is revealed that Ace was planned to have the name of "Portgas D. Lang"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ポートガス・<ruby lang="ja"><rb>D</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ディー</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>・ラング</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Pōtogasu Dī Rangu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> in the early concepts. His looks apparently have not changed much from the original, except for his hat design and the fact that he was supposed to wear sunglasses.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D58&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Ace%27s_Original_Whitebeard_Tattoo.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133123" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Original Whitebeard Tattoo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="68" height="120" data-image-name="Ace's Original Whitebeard Tattoo.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Original_Whitebeard_Tattoo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Ace%27s_Original_Whitebeard_Tattoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/68?cb=20240629133123" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's Whitebeard tattoo as initially drawn in the manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Ace%27s_Original_Whitebeard_Tattoo_Colored.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629133130" class="image"><img alt="Ace's Original Whitebeard Tattoo Colored" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="68" height="120" data-image-name="Ace's Original Whitebeard Tattoo Colored.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_Original_Whitebeard_Tattoo_Colored.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Ace%27s_Original_Whitebeard_Tattoo_Colored.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/68?cb=20240629133130" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's early Whitebeard tattoo fixed in <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Ace%27s_New_Whitebeard_Tattoo.png/revision/latest?cb=20240629134008" class="image"><img alt="Ace's New Whitebeard Tattoo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="109" height="120" data-image-name="Ace's New Whitebeard Tattoo.png" data-image-key="Ace%27s_New_Whitebeard_Tattoo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Ace%27s_New_Whitebeard_Tattoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/109?cb=20240629134008" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's Whitebeard tattoo as drawn later in the manga.
</div></span></div>
<p>Ace's manji is very similar to a swastika. To avoid the manji being mistaken for the Nazi symbol, the Whitebeard tattoo was changed to have crossbones arranged in a cross in the original Japanese anime and later in the manga. This change was also done in the Shonen Jump serialization of the English manga, but was left unedited in the actual volumes. Because of the increase in the number of anime and manga being adapted for sale outside of Japan, this has become a common occurrence among mangaka and publishers alike to avoid the manji symbol.
</p><p>Ace's back tattoo is left intact in the English dub, despite <a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a> previous edits to crosses. At the same time, Ace also promotes his tattoo to Luffy, something which is truly considered odd by 4Kids standards. In the 4Kids version of the anime, Ace's shoulder tattoo signifying his name is edited out, as he is referred to as "Portgaz D. Trace" in it. However, in the TV Funimation dub version it is retained; they reverted his name to the proper "Portgas D. Ace" for the uncut home release. He appears in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Grand_Adventure" title="One Piece: Grand Adventure">One Piece: Grand Adventure</a></i>, once again without the tattoo on his arm.
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>, the early appearances of the tattoo were fixed to match the later ones.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D59&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D60&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Ace appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2012" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2012</a> as one of <a href="/wiki/Chameleone" title="Chameleone">Chameleone</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Kopi_Kopi_no_Mi" title="Kopi Kopi no Mi">transformations</a>. Ace appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show_2017" title="One Piece Premier Show 2017">One Piece Premier Show 2017</a> during the retelling of the events of the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a>. He also appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show_2018" title="One Piece Premier Show 2018">One Piece Premier Show 2018</a> during the retelling of the <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down_Arc" title="Impel Down Arc">Impel Down Arc</a>. Ace is set to appear in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2021" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2021</a>.</li>
<li>A statue of Ace appears in the "Luffy's Endless Adventure" exhibit at <a href="/wiki/Tokyo_One_Piece_Tower" title="Tokyo One Piece Tower">Tokyo One Piece Tower</a>. In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Live_Attraction:_Phantom" title="One Piece Live Attraction: Phantom">One Piece Live Attraction: Phantom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ann" title="Ann">Ann</a> created a <a href="/wiki/Bijo_Bijo_no_Mi" title="Bijo Bijo no Mi">mirage</a> of Ace to help Luffy defeat <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Puggy" title="Puggy">Puggy</a>, and the pirate said a farewell to the show's audience at the end.</li>
<li>Ace appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Dramatic_Stage_THE_METAL_~Marineford_of_Remembrance~" title="One Piece Dramatic Stage THE METAL ~Marineford of Remembrance~">One Piece Dramatic Stage THE METAL ~Marineford of Remembrance~</a> during a flashback of the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>. A statue of Ace was set out on display outside the DMM VR Theatre.</li>
<li>Ace appears in <a href="/wiki/Super_Kabuki_II:_One_Piece" title="Super Kabuki II: One Piece">Super Kabuki II: One Piece</a> during the retelling of the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_Saga" title="Summit War Saga">Summit War Saga</a>.</li>
<li>Ace appears in all four versions of the <a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a> commercials.</li>
<li>A guest comedian on the fifth episode of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Variety:_I_Will_be_the_Pirate_King_TV" title="One Piece Variety: I Will be the Pirate King TV">One Piece Variety: I Will be the Pirate King TV</a> dressed as Portgas D. Ace for a skit.</li></ul>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20201117022541" class="image"><img alt="Ace Premier Show" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="42" height="120" data-image-name="Ace Premier Show.png" data-image-key="Ace_Premier_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Ace_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/42?cb=20201117022541" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace in Premier Show 2019.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Ace_Statue_Tokyo_Tower.png/revision/latest?cb=20201117024107" class="image"><img alt="Ace Statue Tokyo Tower" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="75" height="120" data-image-name="Ace Statue Tokyo Tower.png" data-image-key="Ace_Statue_Tokyo_Tower.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Ace_Statue_Tokyo_Tower.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/75?cb=20201117024107" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Ace's statue in Tokyo One Piece Tower.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D61&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png/revision/latest?cb=20121226162820" class="image"><img alt="Whitebeard and Ace's Graves at Universal Studios Japan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="280" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Whitebeard and Ace's Graves at Universal Studios Japan.png" data-image-key="Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20121226162820"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png/revision/latest?cb=20121226162820" class="image"><img alt="Whitebeard and Ace's Graves at Universal Studios Japan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20121226162820" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="280" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Whitebeard and Ace's Graves at Universal Studios Japan.png" data-image-key="Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20121226162820"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Graves_at_Universal_Studios_Japan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Whitebeard and Ace's graves made by Universal Studios of Japan.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Universal Studios of Japan has built a replica of Ace's and Whitebeard's tombs. Ace's epitaph says: "<i>Ace, may your soul be eternal. Your brave soul will always be with us.</i>" This epitaph was also shown in <a href="/wiki/Episode_663" title="Episode 663">Episode 663</a> of the anime.</li>
<li>Ace has had three different pictures in his <a href="/wiki/Bounties/Gallery" title="Bounties/Gallery">Wanted Poster</a> throughout the series: the first in a <a href="/wiki/Episode_101" title="Episode 101">filler episode</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a>; the second in an <a href="/wiki/Episode_461" title="Episode 461">episode</a> of <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a> (originally as an image of the newspaper in the manga); and the third in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine_Vol.2" title="One Piece Magazine Vol.2">second volume</a> of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine" title="One Piece Magazine">One Piece Magazine</a> (taken from <a href="/wiki/Chapter_158" title="Chapter 158">Chapter 158</a>).</li>
<li>Ace being captain of the Spade Pirates is a pun on the "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ace_of_spades" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ace of spades">ace of spades</a>", which is also named the "Death Card", a possible hint at his eventual death.</li>
<li>In the 2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Ace was ranked 8th, 10th, 5th, 6th, 5th again, and 9th, respectively, making him the most popular of the Whitebeard Pirates and also the most popular deceased character in the series.</li>
<li>Had Ace been a girl, he would have been named "Ann".<sup id="cite_ref-Rouge_Names_Ace_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rouge_Names_Ace-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>Ace's birthday would likely have been in February, and he would have been 21 at death had he been born on time.<sup id="cite_ref-Rouge_Names_Ace_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rouge_Names_Ace-6">[6]</a></sup> Instead, he was born in January, and he was 20<sup id="cite_ref-BrotherhoodAge_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BrotherhoodAge-7">[7]</a></sup> because <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Rouge" title="Portgas D. Rouge">his mother</a> held him in her womb for eleven months past his due date in order to protect him from the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, meaning he spent a total of twenty months inside her womb instead of the usual nine.</li>
<li>The conversation between Ace and Garp in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_525" title="Chapter 525">Chapter 525</a> was likely to misdirect the readers into believing that Ace's biological father was <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, due to him being brothers with Luffy, an assumption that was made by the Marines and Ivankov initially. And that meant Garp and Portgas D. Rouge was their shared grandfather and mother respectively. However, in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_550" title="Chapter 550">Chapter 550</a>, Ace's father is revealed to be Gol D. Roger, and in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_558" title="Chapter 558">Chapter 558</a>, it is elaborated on that he and Luffy were not related by blood, but rather their brotherhood was sworn by <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki_(Ceremony)" title="Sakazuki (Ceremony)">sharing drinks</a>.</li>
<li>Ace is the first character with a <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> to die in the series.</li>
<li>Ace's bounty, being at <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>550,000,000 before his death, was the highest amount revealed in the series before the timeskip.</li>
<li>Ace's favorite foods are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ghost_pepper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ghost pepper">Bhut jolokia peperoncino</a> (ghost pepper spaghetti aglio, olio e peperoncino) and bear meat.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>He's currently the only <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">logia user</a> with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D62&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Ace's birthday, January 1, comes from his name since Ace is the first card in the deck.<sup id="cite_ref-birthandheight_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birthandheight-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/SBS_89" class="mw-redirect" title="SBS 89">SBS 89</a>, Oda showed Ace's possible appearances at ages 40 and 60 in two separate timelines.<br style="clear:both;"></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPortgas_D._Ace%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D63&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
